		icon = GFX_FPR_Raise_the_Black_Horde_decision
		allowed = {

		}

		complete_effect = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = FPR_raising_the_army_tt
			set_country_flag = FPR_raised_army_flag
		}
		remove_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						var = FPR_black_army_experience_var
						value = 0.3
						compare = less_than
					}
				}
				FPR_raise_insurgent_army_green = yes
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						var = FPR_black_army_experience_var
						value = 0.3
						compare = greater_than_or_equals
					}
					check_variable = {
						var = FPR_black_army_experience_var
						value = 0.5
						compare = less_than
					}
				}
				FPR_raise_insurgent_army_regular = yes
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						var = FPR_black_army_experience_var
						value = 0.5
						compare = greater_than_or_equals
					}
					check_variable = {
						var = FPR_black_army_experience_var
						value = 0.7
						compare = less_than
					}
				}
				FPR_raise_insurgent_army_seasoned = yes
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						var = FPR_black_army_experience_var
						value = 0.7
						compare = greater_than_or_equals
					}
					check_variable = {
						var = FPR_black_army_experience_var
						value = 0.9
						compare = less_than
					}
				}
				FPR_raise_insurgent_army_veteran = yes
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						var = FPR_black_army_experience_var
						value = 0.9
						compare = greater_than_or_equals
					}
					check_variable = {
						var = FPR_black_army_experience_var
						value = 1
						compare = less_than
					}
				}
				FPR_raise_insurgent_army_expert = yes
			}

				}

			hidden_effect = {

			puppet = FROM

				if = {
					limit = {
						is_ai = yes
					}
					set_politics = {
						ruling_party = libertarian_socialist
						last_election = "2017.4.23"
						election_frequency = 72
						elections_allowed = no
					}
					create_country_leader = {
						picture = "gfx/leaders/GMA/antifa_generic_1.png"
						ideology = left_anarchist
					}
					random_list = {
						seed = random
						30 = {
							set_cosmetic_tag = FPR_anarchist_collective_1
						}
						30 = {
							set_cosmetic_tag = FPR_anarchist_collective_2

	FAF_Put_Pressure_on_the_Dalmatians_decision = {
		visible = {
			tag = FAF
			CRO = {
				exists = yes
				is_puppet = no
			}
			OR = {
				has_completed_focus = FAF_Ally_European_Identitarians
				has_completed_focus = FAF_Towards_one_Europe
				has_completed_focus = FAF_Discard_Aspects_of_Identitarianism
			}
		}
		available = {
			CRO = {
				NOT = {
					has_government = national_socialist
				}
				has_opinion = {
					target = FAF
					value > 10
				}
			}
			DMT = {
				exists = no
			}
		}
		icon = GFX_Dalmatia
		days_remove = 180
		days_re_enable = 60
		cost = 100
		modifier = {
		}
		targeted_modifier = {
			tag = CRO
			national_socialist_drift = 0.1
			stability_weekly = -0.025
		}
		remove_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					CRO = {
						has_stability > 0.33
						national_socialist < 0.33
					}
				}
				CRO = {
					add_stability = 0.1
					add_opinion_modifier = {
						target = FRA
						modifier = protest_action_strong
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					CRO = {
						has_stability < 0.33
						national_socialist < 0.33
					}
				}
				CRO = {
					country_event = {
						id = serbia.27
						days = 30
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					CRO = {
						national_socialist > 0.33
					}
				}
				CRO = {
					set_politics = {
						ruling_party = national_socialist
						last_election = "2017.4.23"
						election_frequency = 72
						elections_allowed = no
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	FAF_demand_spanish_unification_decision = {
		visible = {
			tag = FAF
			has_completed_focus = FAF_Proclaim_the_Empire
			NOT = {
				41 = {
					is_owned_by = FAF
					is_core_of = FAF
				}
			}
		}
		icon = GFX_decision_FAF_Demand_Spanish_Unification
		days_remove = 90
		fire_only_once = yes
		cost = 100
		complete_effect = {
		}
		remove_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					SNS = {
						is_in_faction_with = FAF
					}
				}
				SNS = {
					country_event = {
						#Latin Empire Demands submission
						id = latinist.10
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						SPR = {
							is_in_faction_with = FAF
						}
						SNS = {
							is_in_faction_with = FAF
						}
					}
				}
				SPR = {
					country_event = {
						id = latinist.10
					}
				}
				SNS = {
					country_event = {
						id = latinist.10
					}
				}
			}
			else = {
				declare_war_on = {
					target = RSR
					type = annex_everything
				}
				declare_war_on = {
					target = SPR
					type = annex_everything
				}
				declare_war_on = {
					target = SNS
					type = annex_everything
				}
			}
		}
	}

	FPR_utopia_female_committee_decision = {
		visible = {
			has_completed_focus = FPR_The_Soft_Revolution
		}
		available = {
			has_completed_focus = FPR_Artisinal_Politics
			NOT = {
				has_idea = FPR_female_committee_idea
			}
		}
		icon = generic_political_rally
		ai_will_do = {
			base = 0
		}
		cost = 50
		days_remove = 100
		fire_only_once = no
		complete_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = FPR_minority_committee_idea
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = FPR_minority_committee_idea
					add_idea = FPR_female_committee_idea
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = FPR_welfare_committee_idea
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = FPR_welfare_committee_idea
					add_idea = FPR_female_committee_idea
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = FPR_justice_committee_idea
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = FPR_justice_committee_idea
					add_idea = FPR_female_committee_idea
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = FPR_diplomatic_committee_idea
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = FPR_diplomatic_committee_idea
					add_idea = FPR_female_committee_idea
				}
			}
			else = {
				add_ideas = FPR_female_committee_idea
				custom_effect_tooltip = FPR_utopia_committee_decision_tt
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = FPR_utopia_committee_decisions_ongoing
				}
				custom_effect_tooltip = FPR_utopia_committee_decision_tt3
				add_stability = -0.05
			}
		}
		remove_effect = {
			hidden_effect = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = {
							has_idea = FPR_female_committee_idea
						}
					}
					add_political_power = -25
					set_temp_variable = {
						var = society_development_var_temp
						value = -0.05
					}
					add_society_development = yes
				}
				else = {
					set_temp_variable = {
						var = society_development_var_temp
						value = 0.01
					}
					add_society_development = yes
				}
			}
			effect_tooltip = {
				custom_effect_tooltip = FPR_utopia_committee_decision_tt3
				add_political_power = -25
				set_temp_variable = {
					var = society_development_var_temp
					value = -0.05
				}
				add_society_development = yes
				custom_effect_tooltip = FPR_utopia_committee_decision_tt4
				set_temp_variable = {
					var = society_development_var_temp
					value = 0.01
				}
				add_society_development = yes
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			custom_modifier_tooltip = FPR_utopia_committee_decision_tt2
			society_development_monthly = 0.01
		}
	}

							type = arms_factory
							damage = 5
						}
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					FROM = {
						tag = GER
					}
				}
				FROM = {
					add_stability = -0.1
					random_owned_controlled_state = {
						limit = {
							is_controlled_by = ROOT
							arms_factory > 0
						}
						damage_building = {
							type = arms_factory
							damage = 5
						}
					}
					random_owned_controlled_state = {
						limit = {
							is_controlled_by = ROOT
							arms_factory > 0
						}
						damage_building = {
							type = arms_factory
							damage = 5
						}
					}
					random_owned_controlled_state = {
						limit = {
							is_controlled_by = ROOT
							arms_factory > 0
						}
						damage_building = {
							type = arms_factory
							damage = 5
						}
					}
					random_owned_controlled_state = {
						limit = {
							is_controlled_by = ROOT
							arms_factory > 0
						}
						damage_building = {
							type = arms_factory
							damage = 5
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
